# The Fall of Tokyo (Shocker)
news_event = {
	id = rksnews.7
	title = rksnews.7.t
	desc = rksnews.7.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_ruins
	
	major = yes
	
	trigger = {
		282 = { is_controlled_by = SHC }
		282 = { is_owned_by = RJP }
		RJP = { has_war_with = SHC }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = fall_of_tokyo_shc }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = fall_of_tokyo_shc
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rksnews.7.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				TAG = SHC
				TAG = GER
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rksnews.7.b
		trigger = { TAG = SHC }
	}
	option = {
		name = rksnews.7.c
		trigger = { TAG = GER }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rksplus.1000
	title = rksplus.1000.t
	desc = rksplus.1000.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_rksplus_startup
	
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	

	option = {
		name = rksplus.1000.a
		
		trigger = { }
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = rksplus_startup_event.1.tt
		set_global_flag = rksplus_startup_event
		
		GER = {
			set_country_flag = GER_rksplus_startup_event_enable
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rksplus.1000.b
		
		trigger = { }
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100

		}

		custom_effect_tooltip = rksplus_startup_event.2.tt
		set_global_flag = rksplus_startup_event
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rksplus.1
	title = rksplus.1.t
	desc = rksplus.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_speech
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	

	option = {
		name = rksplus.1.a
		
		trigger = { country_exists = RGC }
		
		RGC = {
			transfer_state = 731
			
			hidden_effect = {
			add_state_core = 731
			}
		}
		
		GER = { 
		    set_country_flag = GER_macedonia_territorial_decision
		}

	}
	option = {
		name = rksplus.1.b
		
		trigger = { country_exists = RBL }

		RBL = {
			transfer_state = 731
			
			hidden_effect = {
			add_state_core = 731
			}
		}
		
		GER = { 
		    set_country_flag = GER_macedonia_territorial_decision
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rksplus.2
	title = rksplus.2.t
	desc = rksplus.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	

	option = {
		name = rksplus.2.a
		
		trigger = { country_exists = RBM }
		
		GER = {
			annex_country = {
                target = RBM
                transfer_troops = yes
            }
			add_stability = -0.1
			
			hidden_effect = {
			add_state_core = 9
			add_state_core = 75
			add_state_core = 72
			}
			
			set_country_flag = GER_annex_bohemia
		}

	}
}

	id = rksplus.3

country_event = {
	id = rksplus.93
	title = rksplus.93.t
	desc = rksplus.93.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_speech
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	

	option = {
		name = rksplus.93.a

	}
	option = {
		name = rksplus.93.b
		
		trigger = {
		}

		RHG = {
		
		    swap_ideas = {
			    remove_idea = rksplus_germanrule
				add_idea = rksplus_germanrule_collab
			}
			    
		
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = rks_resistance_3
				}
				remove_ideas = rks_resistance_3
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = rks_resistance_2
				}
				remove_ideas = rks_resistance_2
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = rks_resistance_1
				}
				remove_ideas = rks_resistance_1
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = rks_resistance_victory
				}

	id = rksplus.125
	title = rksplus.125.t
	desc = rksplus.125.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_nazis_in_danzig
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rksplus.125.a
		
		trigger = { }

		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism 
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		143 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = arms_factory 
						size > 1
						include_locked = yes
					
						building = dockyard
						size > 1
						include_locked = yes
					}
				}
				
				
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 5
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dockyard 
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes 
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex 
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes 
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = anti_air_building 
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes 
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = air_base 
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes 
				}
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = naval_base
				province = 21
				level = 8
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = coastal_bunker
				province = 21
				level = 6
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 3
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_manpower = 300000
			set_victory_points = {
				province = 21
				value = 10
			}
			set_state_category = large_town
		}
		
		build_railway = {
			path = { 21 3022 }
		}
		
		GER = { set_country_flag = GER_rksplus_nordstern_flag }

	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rksunited.40
	title = rksunited.40.t
	desc = rksunited.40.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rksunited.40.a
		
		trigger = {
		}
		
		RUK = {
			
			hidden_effect = {
				
				add_state_core = 113
				add_state_core = 134
				add_state_core = 119
				add_state_core = 135

				if = {
					limit = {
						RIE = { controls_state = 932 }
					}
					932 = { add_core_of = RIE }
				}
				

			}
			
			annex_country = {
                target = RIE
                transfer_troops = yes
            }
			RIE = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = RUK
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					RUK = {
						has_country_flag = RUK_king_collaboration
					}
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = RUK_united_kingdom_ireland
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					RUK = {
						has_country_flag = RUK_collaboration_bfc_flag
					}
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = RUK_collaboration_bfc_united
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					RUK = {
						has_country_flag = RUK_collaboration_oswald_flag
					}
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = RUK_collaboration_oswald_united
			}
			
			set_country_flag = GER_british_isles_unification_decision
		}
	
    }
	
	option = {
		name = rksunited.40.b
		
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				RIE = {
					has_country_flag = RIE_ireland_collaboration_flag
				}
			}
		}
		
		RUK = {
			
			hidden_effect = {
				
				add_state_core = 113
				add_state_core = 134
				add_state_core = 119
				add_state_core = 135		
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						RIE = { controls_state = 932 }
					}
					932 = { add_core_of = RIE }
				}

			}
			
			annex_country = {
                target = RIE
                transfer_troops = yes
            }
			RIE = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = RUK
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Friedrich Paulus"
				desc = ""
				picture = "gfx/leaders/GER/Portrait_Germany_Friedrich_Paulus.dds"

country_event = {
	id = rkspeacedeal.1
	title = rkspeacedeal.1.t
	desc = rkspeacedeal.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_tanks_snow
	
	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		has_war_with = GER
		surrender_progress > 0.70
		has_civil_war = no
		
		GER = {
			has_government = fascism
			controls_state = 219
			controls_state = 217
			controls_state = 195
		}
	} 

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 20 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	#Surrender and offer territory
	option = {
		name = rkspeacedeal.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = { id = rkspeacedeal.2 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = rkspeacedeal.1.a_tt
		effect_tooltip = {
			GER = {
				add_stability = 0.05
				add_war_support = 0.05
				
				white_peace = {
					tag = SOV
				}
				
				#add_ideas = GER_eastern_chaos
			}
		}
	}

	#Never give up!
	option = {
		name = rkspeacedeal.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0

		}
	}
}

	id = rkspeacedeal.2
	title = rkspeacedeal.2.t
	desc = rkspeacedeal.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_troops
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rkspeacedeal.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_war_support = 0.05
		
		white_peace = SOV
		
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = SOV
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}

			country = SOV
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
			}
			
			white_peace = SOV
		}
		
		SOV = {
			set_capital = {
				state = 653
				remember_old_capital = yes
			}
		
		
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = rksplusussr.1
					days = 90
				}
			}
		}

		#add_ideas = GER_eastern_chaos

			# POL
